Protractor is a reliable framework specifically designed to test Angular and AngularJS applications. This tool simply combines diverse technologies like **Webdriver, Selenium,** and **NodeJS.** ## How Protractor Works Protractor runs numerous tests against your **AngularJS** applications by analyzing the elements and precisely uses Webdriver to control the browser with user actions. If you are thinking about the testing of non-AngularJS applications, Protractor won't disappoint you! One can eventually test the non-AngularJS applications without any glitches. ## The Difference between traditional Selenium Webdriver and Protractor There were certain glitches that occurred while testing an application on the conventional Selenium Webdriver. Here are some aspects associated with Protractor that you should know. - **It exports global function element** that eventually takes the locater and returns _ElementFinder._ This helps in reducing the element locating syntax. - **New Locator approaches** to locate the Angular elements. These strategies include _By.repeater, By.model, By.binding, WebElement.all,_ etc. - You need not add manual **waits to your script.** Protractor ingeniously waits for the loading of the elements. Once the elements are loaded, the next steps are executed. ## How you can be benefitted from Protractor? _Here is the list of features that Protractor offers you:_ 1. **You need not include waits/sleeps** The conventional testing demands he manual waits and sleep, which isn't required in case of Protractor. This can be the best thing from the business point of views as it saves ample time of the professional, which can be utilized in some other productive ways. 1. **Hassle-free syntax for writing test cases** For the users that think that writing huge and complex test cases squanders their time; Protractor has the right solution for the same! One need not write complicated syntax rather needs to write simple syntax to test different Angular applications. 1. **Adequately support the Jasmine/Mocha** Protractor gives you complete support for frameworks like Jasmine and Mocha, which was a shortcoming in the conventional testing tool like Selenium. Thus; it is always a rewarding decision to switch to Protractor for efficient testing solutions. 1. **Easy synchronization and you need not face issues with Angular websites** Most of the application testing professional always face glitches when it comes to the synchronization with the websites made in Angular. Protractor covers this issue and offers easy synchronization with these websites. 1. **Can run the same code even on mobile browsers** Sometimes it becomes quite challenging for individual testing professionals to run the code on the mobile browsers that they earlier tested on their computers. Protractor solves this dilemma and one can run the same code on mobile browsers as well. 1. **Supports almost every web browser** One can now run their test cases on almost every browser and there is no need to install only a specific web browser. 1. **You can use Jasmine and Mocha as the test frameworks for Protractor** Most of the people would be baffled regarding the choice of framework. Well, Protractor efficiently supports BDD (Behavior-Driven Development) test frameworks that enhance its overall reliance. **Jasmine:** You can use the _Jasmine_ **,** which is the default framework when you install Protractor. One can organize and create tests and the user's expectations. The compatibility of Jasmine with protractor makes it possible to extract resources from the browser, which can be further used as promises. **Mocha:** This is a test framework entirely based on JavaScript that runs on NodeJS. If you are planning to use Mocha as the default test framework, you have to set it up with Protractor. This would eventually require the Behavior Driven Development interface along with Chai Assertions. **Downloading Node.js:** Node.js is a cross-platform and open source runtime environment for networking applications. You need to visit the official website to download Node.js. Follow the instructions while you are executing the downloaded file that would set up the Node.js on your PC/laptop. You can check the system variables to verify the installation. Moreover, you can also check from the command prompt by using the command "npm-version" that would display the installed version. Once it is installed, it is the time to move further towards the installation of Protractor. ### Some Advanced Features of Protractor that you should know 1. **Comparing Web Element with a Value:** One can get a **web element** and can indeed compare it with a _certain value._ This feature is beneficial for small and medium businesses that require testing multiple AngularJS applications. One can schedule the comparison on the protractor control flow. This will be executed once all the values are available. 1. **Run your Test Cases in Multiple Browsers** One can easily run their test cases in numerous browsers by using a test script. You can always run your cases in different browsers like Chrome and Firefox. Once you run the configuration file, you would witness the test running in both the browsers. It Protractor utilizes the Selenium grid to run multiple browsers simultaneously. This is again an added advantage that helps in enhancing the overall experience of a developer while testing different cases. 1. **Page Objects can improve your Framework** You can always expect out of the box functionality with this tool when you combine it with POM (Page Object Model). This POM model eventually shuns any of the inadequacies and maintains the overall structure of the project. Protractor simplifies to set up the page objects. Moreover, the tool does not perform any of the Webdriver commands without the need of an action. This simply means that a user can operate the page elements without the need to move HTML. 1. **Capture a screenshot of each test** One can get the numerous reporting packages with Node Package Manager that can help you in capturing the screenshot of every test step. Apart from this, you would get an HTML report regarding the same generated. One just needs to install the packages by using the specific commands in the command prompt. 1. **Precise Integration with tools like Jenkins, Git, Grunt, and BrowserStack** ** ** One can augment their test cases with Protractor as this tool lets you integrate powerful tools like Jenkins, Git, Grunt, and Browserstack efficiently. **Jenkins:** For all those SMBs out there that are unaware about Jenkins; it is a powerful tool that can help you in scheduling your test cases without any hassle. You can use them whenever you need. Apart from this, one can configure the Protractor scripts with Jenkins. It is perhaps the best way to speed up your test cases and can run several test cases at a time. You can also check out some incredible and [beneficial features of Jenkins](https://www.bugraptors.com/use-jenkins-tool-software-testing-features/). **Git:** A powerful tool that can help you in keeping your code at a common storage that can be accessed by multiple developers. This tool is beneficial for the multiple developers that are working on a single project. This tool's integration with Protractor is the game changer as per the experts. **Grunt:** Grunt is another helpful integration for Protractor, which is actually a JavaScript task runner that offers several options for application testing. This tool has surprisingly 4000 tasks and one can even add more tasks as per the needs. This way one can enhance the efficiency of Protractor and eventually get more out of it. **BrowserStack:** When it comes to multiple testing on different browsers, you can always rely on BrowserStack, which is a cross-platform tool for testing your applications. Furthermore, you can quickly integrate BrowserStack with Protractor for efficient results without squandering your precious time. ### Conclusion: No matter if you are an individual developer or a bunch of talented professionals, Protractor is a unique tool that is designed to simplify your work especially for small and medium businesses. You can get the benefits of Selenium as well as get some advanced features that efficiently work with AngularJS applications. ![_config.yml]({{ site.baseurl }}/images/config.png) The easiest way to make your first post is to edit this one.
